---
title: UN/ECE Recommendation N°20 and UN/ECE Recommendation N°21 — Unit codes
description: Code specifying units of measurement.
---

### Codelist [toc]

```ts
import {
	UNIT,
	Unit,
	unitCode,
	PUBLISHED,
	type UnitDefinition,
	type UnitCode,
} from "node-zugferd/codelist/unit";

```
